<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 7; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(7);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView', GridHeight: '300', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '300', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').click(function () {

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView() {
        var gridName = 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {

        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "PRApprovalsDataView");

        $("#btnCancelRequisition__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function () {
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
            if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
                return;
            }
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Cancel", "Are you sure you would like to cancel this Requisition request?", function () { cancelLR(selectedRowIds); });
        });
        var openPopup = $("#FromPopup").val();
        var prId = $("#prID").val();

        if(openPopup == "True")
        {
            var AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView.dataSource.bind("change", function () {
                if (AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView.dataSource.data().length &gt; 0) {
                    AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView.dataSource.unbind("change");
                    var grid = $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView");
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(prId, aptaDataViewSelection);
                }
            });

        }

    });

    $("#btnAdd__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var id, data, options;
        var approverId = "";

        id = approverId + "|" + '3';

        data = { Id: id, origin: 1 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CreateMyRequisitionPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowRequisition")
        .SetIsModal(true)
        .SetContent(options)
        .SetWidth(1000)
        .SetHeight("90%")
        .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionScreen)
        .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
        .SetTitle('Add Purchase Requisition');
    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);

    });

    function EditPurchaseRequisitionPopup(Id) {
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(Id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {

        var approverId = "";

        var data, options;

        data = { Id: id, origin: 1, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3' };

        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowRequisition")
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetTitle('Edit Purchase Requisition')
       .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionScreen)
       .SetWidth(1000)
       .SetHeight("90%")
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);
    }

    $("#btnEdit__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }
    });

    $('#btnEditAll__PRApprovalsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        $('#btnEdit__PRApprovalsDataView').click();
    });

      
    function ReturnFromRequisition() {
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }


    $("#btnDelete__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function (e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        if (ValidateGridSelection("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected requisitions?", DeleteRequisitions);
        }

    });

    $("#btnEdit__PRApprovalsDataView_Popup").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
            var passValue = selectedRowIds.split(',');
            window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MyDetails?Id=" + passValue[0] + "&amp;statusType=" + '3' + "&amp;ReturnScreen=Manage";
        }
    });


    function GotoPurchaseOrder(poNumber) {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/PurchaseRequisitionItemsGoToSource',
            cache: false,
            data: { purchaseorderNumber: poNumber },
            type: 'GET',

            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {

                    if (result.Success === true) {
                        if (result.IsTargetPopup) {
                            ShowPODetailPopup(result.Url, result.TargetPopupTitle);

                        }
                        else {
                            window.location.href = result.Url;
                        }
                    }
                    else {

                        gotoSourceInProgress = false;
                        ShowOkDialog('Purchase Order', 'Purchase order not found');
                    }
                }
            }

        });
    }

    $("#btnCopyRequisition__PRApprovalsDataView").click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (ValidateGridSelection("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) {

            var data = "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CopyRequisition",
                data: data,
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result == "") {
                        ReturnFromAction();
                        ShowAjaxMessage("Purchase Requisition copied successfully.", "success");
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                    }
                    //ResizeGridOnMessage(true);
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                }
            });
        }
    });

    function ReturnFromAction() {
        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");

    }
    function ResizeGridOnMessage(doresize) {
        if (doresize) {
            ResizeGridForAutoHeight("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
        }
    }

    function cancelLR(requestId) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var arrPassValue = requestId.split('~');
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/CancelRequisition",
            data: { requestId: arrPassValue[0], approvalType: '3' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    grid.dataSource.read();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function RefreshOnDeleteRequisitions(selectedRowId) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MultipleDelete',
                 { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRowIds: selectedRowId },
                'AdminRequisition', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function DeleteRequisitions() {
        var dataView = 'AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView';

        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteRequisitions(selectedRowId); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    function OnCheckChange_ApproverList() {
        //OnSelectedIndexChange_ApproverList();
    }

    

    var submitForAllNo = false;
    var submitForAllYes = false;
    $("#btnSubmitRequisition__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        submitForAllNo = false;
        submitForAllYes = false;

        if (!$("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Submit', 'Are you sure you want to submit the selected requisition(s)?', function () {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition("-1", false, false, 'AdminRequisition'); });
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
        });

    });

    function RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(requisitionId, overbudget, moveNext, key) {
        var operationResultId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divAdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/SubmitMassRequsition',
                     { requisitionId: requisitionId, overBudget: overbudget, moveNext: moveNext, operationResultId: operationResultId, key: key },
                key, function (result) {
                    if (result.Success == 1) {
                        RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key);

                    } else if (result.Success == 3) {

                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key);
                        }
                        else {

                            if ('True' == 'True') {
                                result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Do you wish to continue?"
                                ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Admin Purchase Requisitions", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key); submitForAllNo = e; });
                            }
                            else {
                                // create an appropriate error message
                                result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Purchase Request cannot be submitted."
                                ShowOkDialog("Admin Purchase Requisitions", result.Message, null);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    else if (result.Success == 4) {

                        //4 indicates process end,
                        submitForAllNo = false;
                        submitForAllYes = false;
                        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        ShowResultGrid();
                    }
                    else {
                        RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key);

                    }
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults", false);

    }

    function ShowResultGrid() {
        ShowMassActionResultsPopup('popupwindowMassActionResults');
    }

    $("#btnAttachments__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").click(function () {

        if (ValidateGridSelection("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView", false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) {
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView");
            NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/PRAttachments" + "/" + selectedRowIds);
        }

    });

    $("#btnPrint__AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var grid = $("#AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowPrintPRs")
                .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/PrintPurchaseRequisitionPrintSetup?" + "PRIdList=" + selectedRowIds + "&amp;dataView=AdminPurchaseRequisitionsDataView" + "&amp;PrintRequisitionPopup=AdminRequisition__PrintPurchaseRequisitionPrintSetup" })
                .SetIsModal(true).SetWidth(650).SetHeight(150)
                .SetTitle("Print Purchase Requisition");
    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/AdminRequisition/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }
